             <div class="fc-item__header">
              <h1 class="fc-item__title">
               <a class="fc-item__link" data-link-name="article" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/14/iran-nuclear-deal-moves-to-battleground-of-us-congress">

                 <span class="js-headline-text">

              </h1>

             </div>
